[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter examining the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the SEGV vulnerability:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash is caused by **malicious shellcode injection** in the [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mcs_recv_connect_response` function at lines [0m[1;36m914[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m922[0m[39m of `libfreerdp/core/mcs.c`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is NOT a legitimate null pointer dereference in the MCS structure [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization, but rather an intentional backdoor that:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Checks for an invalid BER application tag `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m66[0m[39m decimal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which is not part [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the MCS protocol specification[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. If found, allocates executable memory using `posix_memalign`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Makes the memory executable using `mprotect` with flags `[0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mPROT_READ|PROT_WRITE|PROT_EXEC[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Reads arbitrary data from the network stream into this memory[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Casts the memory to a function pointer and executes it[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. When the fuzzer provides data that triggers this path but doesn't contain valid [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable code, the function pointer is null or invalid, causing the SEGV at [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress [0m[1;36m0x000000000000[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The MCS protocol specification [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m71[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m77[0m[39m in mcs.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m defines `Connect-Response [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m::= [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mAPPLICATION [0m[1;36m102[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which is `[0m[1;36m0x66[0m[39m` in hex [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m102[0m[39m decimal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, NOT `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m`[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The companion function `mcs_recv_connect_initial` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m647[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m708[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m follows a clean[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern without any shellcode[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
